                    --      NDECIMAL --                                         
            EXTERNAL used as    1 2 3   3 EXTERNAL FRED   to build a        para
meter block that will be transfered to the external         routine FRED. Each e
lement in the para block corresponds to a   an integer which is either a value, 
or a pointer if the         command requires one ( signified by the  ). SEE FIRM
 9.6       When the word executes it will find and call the command.       FRED 
may then build values into the para block using ' FRED etc( EXTERNAL COMMAND STR
ING PARAMETERS                29/08/85 )   STRING.DESCR BUILDS 3 ALLOT DOES ( re
turn address )                                                                  
      STRING.DESCR PAD$                                                $" ( --- 
 put string delimited by " to PAD and set PAD$ up )     34 TEXT PAD COUNT PAD$ C
! PAD$ 1+ !                                                                     
                    SETPAD$ ( makes PAD$ point to PAD ) PAD 1+ PAD$ 1+ !        
  SETPAD ( update PAD from PAD$ ) PAD 1+ PAD$ C -TRAILING              SWAP 1 - 
C!                    S                      If a parameter consists of a string
 reference then the          pointer points to a 3 byte string descriptor.      
             PAD$ above is an example. $ takes the word following $          and
 puts it at pad setting up the descriptor as well.                              
                                             Integer pointers may be accessed vi
a variables.                 ( SERIAL PROM SUPPORT                           29/
